FNV PBR PPLIGHTING TEXTURE WRITER CALLSITE DEEP AUDIT

Purpose:
1. Deep-audit the two producer callsites that call FUN_00B68660 and FUN_00B66640.
2. Recover ECX/stack arguments for the texture-array writer and flag initializer.
3. Inspect resolver slot +0x90 usage before assigning BGSTextureSet/PBR texture semantics.
